What a nice find! Just down the street from my work. What a nice experience to be able to go to a taqueria, request a slight change to the menu item ordered (extra cheese, less meat on the quesadilla), and they were so happy to make it how I requested. <Rate>5< /Rate>< review>
Just went in here for the first time on a whim. Wow - so tasty. We got the iced Vietnamese coffee - strong and YUMMY. The owner's cousin makes the macarons. OMG. I have had macarons from bakeries all over Europe - I know what they are supposed to be like. This guy knows how to make them perfectly- they are shiny and slightly crisp as you bite into them and then chewy inside. They are round like they should be with little "feet" - If you know macarons, you know what I mean. Flavors are nice and not too sweet. I'm officially impressed and you will be as well. We weren't hungry for the banh mi, but he gave us a sample of the baguettes they would go on and they are really good - nice and chewy.<//review>

This is liquor store is around my work/play/stomping ground area. This is my emergency "don't go empty handed to a party" liquor store. I enjoy craft Sarsaparilla or regular root beer craft sodas sold here. Only watch out for loquitos in the area so don't leave keys in car or stuff in plain view because you can be in here for a while looking at the selection. When summer was at it's peak I loved going into their walk-in cooler and pretend I couldn't make up my mind on what beer to get.</Review>

< text>
If you've been to this Bar before, you will be pleasantly surprised to discover the new and improved Old 80 BBQ & Bar ( formerly the FLINN BAR). This establishment has been in this location for over 35 yrs...changed owners a few times. They're remodelled inside, & out, especially the back area, with nice private social areas for hanging out with your friends. Food is also very good, BBQ sauce is excellent, @ very moderately priced. We live close by and will definitely be a frequent stop for dinners & Sunday breakfasts that people are talking about.</text>

This really should have two ratings:
Bar: 3.5 stars
Grill: 1.5 stars
This is one of those places that you probably will either really like or not go back. The food was luke-warm. The portions were good size, fair price. They switched from tap to can for my beer selection and didn't tell me. Can vs Tap? Really? Seems like a heads up would be in order, especially if you consider yourself a bar.
You'll like it if you fit the demographic, want a bar with edible food,  have reason to be in the area and are over 50 (yeah, I know that is technically a demographic, but it is worth calling out).
You won't like it if you want better than average BBQ (can‚Äôt compare to Coops in Lemon Grove, Iron Pig Ale House in PB... I'd say even Dickie's has better BBQ. Which Coops was closer/easier to get to), want something other than an IPA, know the difference between Scotch and Whiskey, want hot food, mind blowing sides, have to make a special trip to get there, aren't a hipster but can spot one. (I'd pay to read a review of this place from a hipster btw)
Strangely, since I drive that area often, I can see myself dropping in again, giving them at least one more try. Can‚Äôt really recommend it, but I‚Äôve had worse. They do have Guinness‚Ä¶< /Review>

<user_id>111023986332135746257</user_id><Text>We are long time customers of the former restaurant and very familiar with the previous menu and the location. 3 of the 5 in our party are in the food & bar industry, so we're not harsh but know how things work. Maybe the staff was short handed or maybe overwhelmed, either way? Our brunch visit yesterday, mehh...

WAIT STAFF - 4 stars
Our server was very friendly, greeted us promptly, took our orders and continued to check in on us. She explained the delays in our Bar order, delays in completing our food order and agreed about the quality of the pork in a dish. While we had some issues with the items ordered being accurate, she still wins for attitude and attentiveness.

BAR SERVICE - 1 Star
Slow; First of 2 Mimosas we ordered? The wineglass had LIPSTICK plainly visible on the rim, and food particles on the inside of the glass. WE took it back to the bar, complained about the lipstick. The Pineapple Mimosa that was returned to us? Smaller red wine glass and was not a Pineapple Mimosa, didn't taste like the other Pineapple Mimosa ordered. Our party didn't try for a number 3 and just drank this one. $5 is a decent price. $8 Bloody Mary was pretty good, came with salted rim even though it is "upon request". .
Note, our server had to wait for the bar staff on several occasions, returning to tell us she hadn't forgotten but was waiting on our cocktails.

FOOD - 2.5 stars
This one is where they really fell down in consistency, menu accuracy and quality. Menu prices are average and as expected, with a decent variety.
The new menu has a Tri-tip Scramble and a Pulled Pork Scramble.
We will NOT ORDER these again. Both came with large chunks of re-heated meat and it wasn't hot. Pork is described in the menu as "shredded" pulled pork...nope. 1" cubes of re-heated pork and not well-trimmed. Our diner pulled them all to the side, totally unappetizing.
Biscuits and Gravy came out with 1 split biscuit & gravy and 2 slices bacon (?) B&G item doesn't come with bacon and that costs the kitchen money. The gravy is a solid 4 and a lot like the former recipe.
The Old 80 was served with Biscuit & Gravy (not ordered that way) and Toast.
The Monterey Jack cheese used on the Veggie Omelet is processed Jack cheese slice, not actual Monterey Jack.
Solid food items? The gravy and the eggs were all prepared correctly. Home fries are tasty, but weren't hot all the way through.

NOTE THAT when we complained to our server about the pork and she saw it wasn't eaten, she agreed with us and commented she had already spoken to the kitchen staff earlier with another complaint about the very same issue. We didn't expect to get that meal compd, but speaking to a manager or getting an invite to return and try it again after the bar issue and food? Nope, didn't happen.

DECOR / AMBIANCE - 5 stars
This is the only things that brings up the stars. The new owners did a nice job of updating the back outdoor area. It really looks great with 2 cabanas that are well-appointed for groups. They updated everything, adding new roof, adding a stage, a walk-up bar (not staffed yesterday), new paint, etc.. The interior is also updated and very inviting. Plenty of parking too.
If they can get the F&B together, I would absolutely book the outdoor area for a private party. It's well done.

OVERALL, we spent $96 for 5 people, before tip.
We won't be going back anytime soon, and that's sad. We hope the new owner listens to the reviews, because we would go back just for the ambiance, if they can correct these F&B issues.</Text>< gmapID>

< review>
I'm sorry to see this place has such negative reviews, but I understand some of the frustrations. The place DOES seem understaffed, which is not the fault of the folx working at the counter. I have yet to have anything but a positive experience with any of the employees, and, in fact, have one employee in particular I look forward to seeing every time I come in. This place is incredibly busy at certain times, and I feel many people waiting in line take out their frustrations on the PO staff, at least in terms of reviews. It's a hard case all around, made worse by what is being done to the USPS at the federal level.

As for deliveries, I have yet to have a package go missing or arrive damaged on either end of my transactions here. I have had some personal packages arrive late, but that was absolutely the fault of the outgoing PO rather than this one.

Just wanted to suggest that not all experiences here are terrible ones; even on my worst days, I've made the best of it. Going to the PO has always been a chore I despise as it is, and it's nice for me to have a place I don't mind going.<//review>

< Review>
My Husband and I moved from Idaho in Feb to California. We researched a good storage option, and decided on North Main Street Storage and booked a package through THEIR website. Well when we got there from our 2 day drive from Idaho with all of our things, we show up to the storage unit only to be harassed by the manager (Diana, her name is everywhere. I couldn't forget it if I tried) telling us that the special we had email proof that we received "doesn't exist" and she tried to bully us into paying the full $190 a month for the unit-- which I of course refused and told her she would honor the $80 deal we received. She agreed to do that for 4 months and would put notes into the system so we didn't get charged the full amount. So we moved into our unit.

The following month I called in 4 days before rent was due to pay-- she couldn't find her notes and was insisting I needed to pay the $190 rent. I refused and told her to keep looking. Diana eventually remembered our interaction the month prior so she allowed us to pay the prorated rent and assured me that she would make sure to have notes on our account this time. Then 2 weeks later while in Texas visiting family I get a call from my mother telling me that we got a letter from our storage place and asked if she should open it, I agreed. The letter was a threat for not "paying full rent" telling us they were going to lock us out of our unit if it wasn't paid within a few days. I was livid and called North Main Storage only to get Diana. She tried to convince me I was wrong AGAIN. Then after 20 mins on the phone "found her notes" and assured me we wouldn't be kicked out of our unit.

The following month we were still in Texas (thanks Covid), so I called to pay our rent again. Only to do the exact same thing as the previous month-- down to the threatening letter to remove us from the unit for partial rent.

The 4th and final month we were in our unit, I asked my husband to call and deal with Diana because I was DONE. Of course he calls and gets wonderful, easy going and competent Kenny (couldn't say better things about this guy, he was awesome.) So within 2 mins Kenny found Diana's note about our account and my husband paid for our final month-- no issues.

Then during the 4th and final month my husband and I flew into CA after covid restrictions were lifted to clean out our unit and move our belongings. The first 2 days we were clean it out we had wonderful Kenny, so we weren't harassed. Then on the 3rd day we showed up at 9:10 to our unit (it was supposed to be unlocked by 9am btw) and the units are still locked.
